# Skyrim:Mightier than the Sword

## Overview

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read [Looter's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Looter%27s_Note "Skyrim:Looter's Note") in [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") of Markarth
2. Search the tower at [Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie").
3. Pick up the leftover loot.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This quest can be started by heading to the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") within [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). Go inside and find the *[Looter's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Looter%27s_Note "Skyrim:Looter's Note")* left by a patron upon the bar counter. Now head to [Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie"), a Dwemer tower southeast of Markarth and northeast of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"). Upon arrival, three [Looters](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Looter&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Looter (page does not exist)") will begin attacking. Go inside the tower and go up the steps. At the top will be the body of dead Dark Elf named [Casival](/wiki/Skyrim:Casival "Skyrim:Casival"). Loot him to find a copy of *[The Crimson Dirks, v9](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v9 "Skyrim:The Crimson Dirks, v9")*. On the table and ground you will find the two pieces of [Dwarven Plate Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven#Dwarven_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Dwarven") and *[Casival's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Casival%27s_Note "Skyrim:Casival's Note")*.

## Bugs

- The Looter's note may be clipped into the bar. **?**
  - Using a spell that has knockback seems to work. For example, Fire Storm, Elemental Burst and Fireball may work. The illusion spell Harmony also works if you do not want to kill the patrons or make them hostile to you.
- If you have already visited Reachwind Eyrie and picked up the Dwarvern Plate armor, you will not be able to complete the quest.
  - Dropping it back in Reachwind Eyrie before activating the quest prevents this.
  - If you have already activated the quest, are in Reachwind Eyrie, and the Armor is now marked as a quest item try the console command:  `drop xx027800 1`  (where xx is the load order - usually fe) then pick up the armor.
  - Re-acquiring the Dwarven Plate armor in Reachwind Eyrie, through a trade can also fix the quest.
  - If you've already sold the Dwarven Plate Armor or the above suggestions do not work, you can force completion by using the console command: `SetStage ccBGSSSE061_quest 1000`
  - Once completed the Dwarven Plate Boots will no longer be marked as quest items.
- Looters and bandit around and in the Reachwind Eyrie may not spawn upon reaching the area or heading into the tower making it impossible to complete the quest. **?**
- The two quest armor pieces have strange weight behaviors. At one lb. under max weight, picking up the Plate Armor caused no apparent change in weight carried. Picking up the Boots caused the weight from the Armor to be "noticed", but despite now being 44 lbs. overweight, movement speed was unaffected. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Mightier than the Sword (ccBGSSSE061\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Inns across Skyrim are typically a good place to find work. Should I find myself in Markarth, I should stop by the Silver-Blood Inn and see if I can't come across any news or rumors. *Objective 10:* Investigate the Silver-Blood Inn for rumors |
| 20 |  | Inns across Skyrim are typically a good place to find work. I found a note left by a patron at the Silver-Blood Inn that mentions some decent loot might be found at Reachwind Eyrie to the south. *Objective 20:* Search the tower at Reachwind Eyrie |
| 30 |  | Inns across Skyrim are typically a good place to find work. I found a note left by a patron at the Silver-Blood Inn that mentioned some decent loot might be found at Reachwind Eyrie to the south. When I arrived, I was attacked by three looters. At the top of the tower, I found the body of a bandit. *Objective 30:* Pick up the leftover loot |
| 1000 | ☑ | Inns across Skyrim are typically a good place to find work. I found a note left by a patron at the Silver-Blood Inn that mentioned some decent loot might be found at Reachwind Eyrie to the south. When I arrived, I was attacked by three looters. At the top of the tower, I found the body of a bandit and pieces of Dwarven Plate armor. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 40, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE061_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE061_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Military Camps

## Overview

Winterhold Imperial Camp

This page lists all the **military camps** that are established for the [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). [Military forts](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") are listed on a separate page.

### Imperial Camps

:    **[Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Eastmarch, located southeast of Mzulft and north of Stony Creek Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eastmarch+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Falkreath Hold, located east-northeast of Glenmoril Coven and north of Knifepoint Ridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Hjaalmarch, located south of Ustengrav and northwest of Stonehills. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Pale, located west of Dawnstar and northwest of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Reach, located south of Bthardamz and west of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Rift, located south of Ivarstead and west of the Ruins of Bthalft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Whiterun Hold, located east of Rorikstead and far west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Windhelm Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Windhelm Military Camp")** — An Imperial camp set up east of Brandy-Mug Farm for the attack on Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm+Military+Camp)
:    **[Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Winterhold Hold, located southeast of Dawnstar and northwest of Frostflow Lighthouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Imperial+Camp)

### Stormcloak Camps

:    **[Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Falkreath Hold, located east of Helgen. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Haafingar, located northeast of Dragon Bridge and south of the Statue to Meridia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haafingar+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Hjaalmarch, located east of Ustengrav and west of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Pale, located southeast of Bronze Water Cave on the south shore of Lake Yorgrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Reach, located west of Liar's Retreat and northeast of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Rift, located northeast of Sarethi Farm and west of Rift Watchtower. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Solitude Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Solitude Military Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp set up west of Katla's Farm for the attack on Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Military+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Military Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp set up east of Pelagia Farm for the attack on Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Military+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Whiterun Hold, located south of the Ritual Stone and east of White River Watch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Winterhold Hold, located northeast of Windhelm and south of Snow Veil Sanctum. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Stormcloak+Camp)

## Notes

- The three camps that include "Military Camp" in their titles are temporary, established only when your side is the attacker in a siege (Stormcloaks on Whiterun and Solitude; Imperials on Windhelm only, since their role in the Battle of Whiterun is defensive). The "Imperial Camps" and "Stormcloak Camps" are more permanent locations for the side not in control of the hold in question.
- Neither the Imperials nor the Stormcloaks will set up camp in their own former capital's hold: there is no Haafingar Imperial Camp even if the Stormcloaks take Solitude, or Eastmarch Stormcloak Camp even if the Imperials take Windhelm.
- After the Civil War questline is completed, the military camps for the side that prevailed will be disbanded, and their markers will be removed from the world and local maps. However, the local map will still show your location's title as "Imperial Military Camp" or "Stormcloak Military Camp", as appropriate. If one side takes over a hold before the end of the war, the newly controlling faction may disband its camp in that hold and move the soldiers who were at that camp to that hold's capital.
- Although [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf "Skyrim:Balgruuf") is initially neutral, Whiterun Imperial Camp won't be set up unless you [capture Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") for the Stormcloaks.
- Both Winterhold camps are closer to other hold capitals than they are to the [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Winterhold Imperial Camp is closer to [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and Winterhold Stormcloak Camp is closer to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
- Unlike regular blacksmiths, simply talking to the quartermasters at these camps is enough to see what they have for sale.
- Falkreath Stormcloak Camp and Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp both feature a roasted skeever on a campfire that you can harvest for [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"). Every other camp has a [cooking station](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") you can use.
- Calcelmo may [ask for Dwemer items](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact") bought from these camps, sending you a note by courier. The note will state only "military camp" instead of the camp's actual name. For example, Reach Stormcloak Camp and Winterhold Imperial Camp will simply be recognized in the note as "Stormcloak military camp" and "Imperial military camp", respectively.
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") has all of the wounded soldiers at each camp check to see if the field CO at their camp is alive or dead before enabling themselves. But this may be moot even then, since the CO's are always essential, anyway.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks all items and containers at each camp as owned by the camp's respective military faction, regardless whether they were owned beforehand or not.

## Bugs

- When a military camp is disbanded and its war map removed, the map's city and fort markers may remain floating in the air.
- The Imperial legates and Stormcloak officers in their respective camps remain essential once the Civil War questline is finished. **?**

# Skyrim:Military Camps

## Overview

Winterhold Imperial Camp

This page lists all the **military camps** that are established for the [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). [Military forts](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") are listed on a separate page.

### Imperial Camps

:    **[Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Eastmarch, located southeast of Mzulft and north of Stony Creek Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eastmarch+Imperial+Camp)

## Notes

- The three camps that include "Military Camp" in their titles are temporary, established only when your side is the attacker in a siege (Stormcloaks on Whiterun and Solitude; Imperials on Windhelm only, since their role in the Battle of Whiterun is defensive). The "Imperial Camps" and "Stormcloak Camps" are more permanent locations for the side not in control of the hold in question.
- Neither the Imperials nor the Stormcloaks will set up camp in their own former capital's hold: there is no Haafingar Imperial Camp even if the Stormcloaks take Solitude, or Eastmarch Stormcloak Camp even if the Imperials take Windhelm.
- After the Civil War questline is completed, the military camps for the side that prevailed will be disbanded, and their markers will be removed from the world and local maps. However, the local map will still show your location's title as "Imperial Military Camp" or "Stormcloak Military Camp", as appropriate. If one side takes over a hold before the end of the war, the newly controlling faction may disband its camp in that hold and move the soldiers who were at that camp to that hold's capital.
- Although [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf "Skyrim:Balgruuf") is initially neutral, Whiterun Imperial Camp won't be set up unless you [capture Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") for the Stormcloaks.
- Both Winterhold camps are closer to other hold capitals than they are to the [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Winterhold Imperial Camp is closer to [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and Winterhold Stormcloak Camp is closer to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
- Unlike regular blacksmiths, simply talking to the quartermasters at these camps is enough to see what they have for sale.
- Falkreath Stormcloak Camp and Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp both feature a roasted skeever on a campfire that you can harvest for [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"). Every other camp has a [cooking station](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") you can use.
- Calcelmo may [ask for Dwemer items](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact") bought from these camps, sending you a note by courier. The note will state only "military camp" instead of the camp's actual name. For example, Reach Stormcloak Camp and Winterhold Imperial Camp will simply be recognized in the note as "Stormcloak military camp" and "Imperial military camp", respectively.
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") has all of the wounded soldiers at each camp check to see if the field CO at their camp is alive or dead before enabling themselves. But this may be moot even then, since the CO's are always essential, anyway.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks all items and containers at each camp as owned by the camp's respective military faction, regardless whether they were owned beforehand or not.

## Bugs

- When a military camp is disbanded and its war map removed, the map's city and fort markers may remain floating in the air.
- The Imperial legates and Stormcloak officers in their respective camps remain essential once the Civil War questline is finished. **?**

# Skyrim:Military Camps

## Overview

Winterhold Imperial Camp

This page lists all the **military camps** that are established for the [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). [Military forts](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") are listed on a separate page.

### Imperial Camps

:    **[Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Eastmarch, located southeast of Mzulft and north of Stony Creek Cave. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eastmarch+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Falkreath Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Falkreath Hold, located east-northeast of Glenmoril Coven and north of Knifepoint Ridge. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Hjaalmarch, located south of Ustengrav and northwest of Stonehills. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Pale Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Pale, located west of Dawnstar and northwest of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Reach Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Reach, located south of Bthardamz and west of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Rift Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in the Rift, located south of Ivarstead and west of the Ruins of Bthalft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Whiterun Hold, located east of Rorikstead and far west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Imperial+Camp)
:    **[Windhelm Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Windhelm Military Camp")** — An Imperial camp set up east of Brandy-Mug Farm for the attack on Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm+Military+Camp)
:    **[Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp")** — An Imperial camp in Winterhold Hold, located southeast of Dawnstar and northwest of Frostflow Lighthouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Imperial+Camp)

### Stormcloak Camps

:    **[Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Falkreath Hold, located east of Helgen. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Falkreath+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Haafingar, located northeast of Dragon Bridge and south of the Statue to Meridia. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haafingar+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Hjaalmarch, located east of Ustengrav and west of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hjaalmarch+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Pale, located southeast of Bronze Water Cave on the south shore of Lake Yorgrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pale+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Reach, located west of Liar's Retreat and northeast of Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reach+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in the Rift, located northeast of Sarethi Farm and west of Rift Watchtower. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rift+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Solitude Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Solitude Military Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp set up west of Katla's Farm for the attack on Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Military+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Military Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp set up east of Pelagia Farm for the attack on Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Military+Camp)
:    **[Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Whiterun Hold, located south of the Ritual Stone and east of White River Watch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whiterun+Stormcloak+Camp)
:    **[Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp")** — A Stormcloak camp in Winterhold Hold, located northeast of Windhelm and south of Snow Veil Sanctum. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Winterhold+Stormcloak+Camp)

## Notes

- The three camps that include "Military Camp" in their titles are temporary, established only when your side is the attacker in a siege (Stormcloaks on Whiterun and Solitude; Imperials on Windhelm only, since their role in the Battle of Whiterun is defensive). The "Imperial Camps" and "Stormcloak Camps" are more permanent locations for the side not in control of the hold in question.
- Neither the Imperials nor the Stormcloaks will set up camp in their own former capital's hold: there is no Haafingar Imperial Camp even if the Stormcloaks take Solitude, or Eastmarch Stormcloak Camp even if the Imperials take Windhelm.
- After the Civil War questline is completed, the military camps for the side that prevailed will be disbanded, and their markers will be removed from the world and local maps. However, the local map will still show your location's title as "Imperial Military Camp" or "Stormcloak Military Camp", as appropriate. If one side takes over a hold before the end of the war, the newly controlling faction may disband its camp in that hold and move the soldiers who were at that camp to that hold's capital.
- Although [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf "Skyrim:Balgruuf") is initially neutral, Whiterun Imperial Camp won't be set up unless you [capture Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") for the Stormcloaks.
- Both Winterhold camps are closer to other hold capitals than they are to the [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Winterhold Imperial Camp is closer to [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and Winterhold Stormcloak Camp is closer to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
- Unlike regular blacksmiths, simply talking to the quartermasters at these camps is enough to see what they have for sale.
- Falkreath Stormcloak Camp and Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp both feature a roasted skeever on a campfire that you can harvest for [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"). Every other camp has a [cooking station](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") you can use.
- Calcelmo may [ask for Dwemer items](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact") bought from these camps, sending you a note by courier. The note will state only "military camp" instead of the camp's actual name. For example, Reach Stormcloak Camp and Winterhold Imperial Camp will simply be recognized in the note as "Stormcloak military camp" and "Imperial military camp", respectively.
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") has all of the wounded soldiers at each camp check to see if the field CO at their camp is alive or dead before enabling themselves. But this may be moot even then, since the CO's are always essential, anyway.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks all items and containers at each camp as owned by the camp's respective military faction, regardless whether they were owned beforehand or not.

## Bugs

- When a military camp is disbanded and its war map removed, the map's city and fort markers may remain floating in the air.
- The Imperial legates and Stormcloak officers in their respective camps remain essential once the Civil War questline is finished. **?**

# Skyrim:Military Forts

## Overview

Fort Greenwall

 This page lists all the **military forts** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Military camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps") are listed on a separate page.

The locations using the fort map marker can be roughly divided into three types. Forts affected by the **Civil War** appear in the first section. The occupants of these forts are initially bandits and mages. As the [Skyrim Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") progresses, either the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") will take over and occupy the fort.

Forts can serve as **settlements** for factions: the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), and the [Volkihar Vampire Clan](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

Other forts are set up as standard **dungeons**, with respawning enemies and a boss you must kill to clear the dungeon.

### Civil War Forts

:    **[Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol")** — A medium-sized fort southwest of Windhelm initially occupied by warlocks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Amol)
:    **[Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad")** — A large fort south of Dawnstar initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dunstad)
:    **[Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall")** — A large fort north-northwest of Riften initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Greenwall)
:    **[Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor")** — A medium-sized fort west of Whiterun initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Greymoor)
:    **[Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad")** — A medium-sized fort west of Solitude initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Hraggstad)
:    **[Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav")** — A medium-sized fort south of Winterhold initially occupied by warlocks and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Kastav)
:    **[Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad")** — A medium-sized fort east of Falkreath initially occupied by bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Neugrad)
:    **[Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk")** — A medium-sized fort west of Morthal initially occupied by necromancers and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Snowhawk)
:    **[Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard")** — A large fort east-southeast of Markarth initially occupied by Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Sungard)

### Fort Settlements

:    **[Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large castle on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Volkihar Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)

    :   **[Volkihar Courtyard](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Courtyard "Skyrim:Volkihar Courtyard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — The courtyard attached to Castle Volkihar and Volkihar Keep.
    :    **[Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fortress on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Castle Volkihar which serves as the Volkihar vampire clan's home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)
:    **[Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fort southeast of Riften which serves as the Dawnguard's base of operations. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dawnguard+%28DG%29)
:    **[High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar")** — A small settlement southeast of Whiterun roughly halfway up the Throat of the World. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Hrothgar)

### Fort Dungeons

:    **[Ashfallow Citadel](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfallow_Citadel "Skyrim:Ashfallow Citadel")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Imperial fort east of Highpoint Tower and northwest of the Sun Stone being used as a base of operations by the Morag Tong. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Ashfallow+Citadel)
:    **[Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne")** — A small fort southwest of Helgen containing vampires, wolves, gargoyles, and death hounds. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bloodlet+Throne)
:    **[Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt")** — A medium-sized fort east of Karthwasten containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Tower+Redoubt)
:    **[Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep")** — A medium-sized fort west of Falkreath containing Orc bandits and hunters led by Ghunzul. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cracked+Tusk+Keep)
:    **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized fort southwest of Riften containing hagravens, hags, and witches. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
:    **[Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge")** — A medium-sized fort southeast of Dawnstar containing Silver Hands. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Driftshade+Refuge)
:    **[Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth")** — A medium-sized fort west of Riften containing bandits, wolves, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Faldar%27s+Tooth)
:    **[Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep")** — A medium-sized fort east-northeast of Whiterun containing warlocks, atronachs, and vampires, and the mages' leader, the Caller. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fellglow+Keep)
:    **[Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer")** — A medium-sized fort and iron mine south of Dawnstar containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Fellhammer)
:    **[Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small fort south of Highpoint Tower and northeast of Hrodulf's House occupied by ash spawn and General Falx Carius. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Fort+Frostmoth)
:    **[Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock")** — A small fort southwest of Windhelm containing Silver Hands and their leader Krev the Skinner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gallows+Rock)
:    **[Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl")** — A small fort north of Karthwasten containing the warlock Kornalus and his enchanted frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Harmugstahl)
:    **[Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small fort east of Raven Rock containing albino spiders, ash spawn, and Neloth's former apprentice Ildari Sarothril. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Highpoint+Tower)
:    **[Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep")** — A medium-sized fort north of the Lady Stone containing necromancers and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ilinalta%27s+Deep)
:    **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch")** — A medium-sized fort east of Darkwater Crossing containing the Mistwatch Bandits and their leader. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)
:    **[Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar")** — A small fort southwest of Windhelm containing warlocks and their leader Naris the Wicked. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Morvunskar)
:    **[Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple")** — A small fort on the clifftop overlooking Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightcaller+Temple)
:    **[Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep")** — A small fort northwest of Dragon Bridge containing Thalmor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwatch+Keep)
:    **[Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch")** — A medium-sized fort southeast of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva%27s+Watch)
:    **[Western Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Western_Watchtower "Skyrim:Western Watchtower")** — A small fort west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Western+Watchtower)

## Notes

- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks everything new inside and outside of each Civil War fort as owned by the fort's new corresponding faction once the soldiers move in.

# Skyrim:Mine or Yours

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") by ridding the [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") |
| Location(s): | [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"), [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar")) |
| ID: | FreeformShorsStone01 |

Redbelly Mine

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar") about the local mine.
2. Clear [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") of [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").
3. Return to Filnjar.

### Of Sulfur and Spiders

[Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine") is a small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") located in [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). The mine gets its name from the red mist filling the caverns and smelling like the sulfurous hot springs out in the volcanic tundra. The local blacksmith, [Filnjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar "Skyrim:Filnjar"), will tell you the mine is not producing right now. In fact, the mine is currently overrun with [spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Filnjar is worried that the invading arachnids will venture out of the mine looking for food soon. What's worse, the town guards are as useless as "a fifth wheel on a wagon" as they prefer to keep an eye out for enemy soldiers rather than trouble themselves protecting the town's major commodity. If you are willing to give Filnjar a hand, he will tell you, *"Keep to your word, and I'll line your pockets with as much as I can scrape up."*

### Spider Extermination

The mine is to the west, close to [Filnjar's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Filnjar%27s_House "Skyrim:Filnjar's House"). Get into the mine and you'll find some frostbite spiders soon. There are two groups of three spiders, with medium and small spiders attacking en masse. Remove every spider to complete the quest. You can also find the three ebony ore veins near the bottom level of the mine.

### Gold for Spiders

Return to Filnjar and tell him the good news. *"Gone? Every one of them? Why, that's incredible."* Then he'll reward you with leveled gold for reopening the mine and putting Shor's Stone back on the map.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- There is a [Shor's Stone Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone_Guard "Skyrim:Shor's Stone Guard") that sits outside the mine. You can utilize a common bug where they will follow you into the mine while dialogue is ongoing and they can then be used to help clear the mine, though it's not a difficult task unless attempted at a very low level.
- Killing all the frostbite spiders triggers the option to "Return to Filnjar" regardless of having talked to him or not.
- Filnjar's dialogue does not change even if the Civil War is over; he still says the guards are looking out for enemy soldiers.

## Bugs

- This quest does not display a quest pointer as intended due to checking the wrong conditions for the objective alias.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- There are several desiccated corpses within the mine despite Filnjar stating that nobody had been harmed by the infestation.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- After first completion, the spiders may respawn and the miners will continue to work in the newly infested mine, potentially causing harm to NPCs in the mine.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
  - If the spiders respawn and you have already completed the quest once, the quest will reset at the point where you have to return to Filnjar after killing some or all of the spiders, allowing you to repeat the quest as many times as you want.
  - The miners leave the mine at night; entering the mine then should allow you to kill the spiders again without any harm coming to the miners.

## Quest Stages

| Mine or Yours (FreeformShorsStone01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Clear Redbelly Mine of spiders |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Filnjar |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformShorsStone01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformShorsStone01`.

# Skyrim:Mine Ore

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore.** | |

Mining for ore

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following people. Total  in the following table is simply the amount you can obtain by mining all the veins in the quest-giver's mine; more money is possible if you also sell ores collected elsewhere.

[\*](#note_mine)These people will only buy ore from you if you help them reclaim their mines.

[†](#note_ironval)Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") also allows you to sell iron ore to him.

## Walkthrough

If you talk to one of the quest givers, they will offer to pay you for any ore you mine. Each quest-giver will only accept a single type of ore, as listed in the above table. You can also mine ore without talking to a quest giver, and either sell them the ore later or use the ore yourself (e.g., by [smelting](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") it). For most ores you are paid its standard base value, with the exception of Iron Ore, for which you receive 7 gold instead of 2 gold. The amount you are paid is fixed, and does not depend upon your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill or perks. All ore of the specified type will be purchased.

Information on how and where to mine is provided at [Mining](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining").

## Achievements

An [Achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is related to mining ore:

-  **[Hard Worker](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Worker "Skyrim:Hard Worker")** (10 points/Bronze) — [Chop wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood"), [mine ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining"), and [cook food](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking")
  - To obtain this achievement you do not need to sell the ore, or even talk to any of the quest givers. Simply activating an ore vein is sufficient.

## Notes

- This quest does not have any stages or objectives.
- This quest can be repeated indefinitely.
- The dialogue option to sell the ore only appears if you have the specified type of ore in your inventory.
- The quest giver will buy all the ore of the specified type that you are carrying, so if you want to save any, you must remove it from your inventory first.
- Money you earn from mining ore is fixed, and if the ore is sold through direct dialogue rather than the merchant screen, is not affected by your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill. This makes the quest one of the few ways to [make money](/wiki/Skyrim:Making_Money "Skyrim:Making Money") without increasing any skills, which will help control your level. This is useful when wanting to [train](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in a certain skill as many times as possible. It is also one of the few ways to earn money without doing any questing, merchanting, or crafting.
- Completing this quest at Redbelly Mine will raise your favor with the owner, Grogmar, and he will make you [blood-kin to the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") as a result.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.

# Skyrim:Miner's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

| SoljundsSinkholeMinersHouse | |

| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Next to [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole"), North of [Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Old Hroldan") and west of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") | |

Miner's House

The **Miner's House** is a single-room cottage next to [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole").

It is the home of [Tuthul](/wiki/Skyrim:Tuthul "Skyrim:Tuthul") and [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth"), the miners at Soljund's Sinkhole.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Perth](/wiki/Skyrim:Perth "Skyrim:Perth")  [Tuthul](/wiki/Skyrim:Tuthul "Skyrim:Tuthul") |

## Miner's House

The entrance is novice-locked most of the time. Upon entering there is a cupboard against the south wall holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), four loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") and two [sabre cat pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt"), with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel to the right. Against the west wall is a long wooden table with two [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on top. To the right, in the northwest corner is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling above. While against the north wall is another long wooden table with two bottles of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a few loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several pieces of cheese. Hanging from racks above the table are four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). There is a fireplace opposite the entrance with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against a pile of firewood and an unlocked chest to the right of the fireplace. There are two single owned beds coming out from the east wall and an end table between them with a bottle of alto wine and a bottle of wine on top. At the foot of the right-hand bed, against the south wall is a small round wooden table and a chair, with two bottles of alto wine and a loaf of bread on top of the table.

# Skyrim:Mines

## Overview

Embershard Mine

 This page lists all the **mines** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). Mines generally contain several veins of [ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Ores "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots"). Ore veins in uncleared mines, including unclearable mines such as Gloombound Mine, respawn in 10 in-game days, while ore veins in cleared mines respawn in 30 in-game days. For details on how to mine ore and lists of where various ores can be found, see [Mining](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining").

:    **[Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine")** — A small orichalcum mine northwest of Falkreath containing Orc bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bilegulch+Mine)
:    **[Broken Tusk Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tusk_Mine "Skyrim:Broken Tusk Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small heart stone mine north of Raven Rock containing rieklings. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Broken+Tusk+Mine)
:   **[Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")** — A medium-sized silver mine and forced-labor prison camp in southern Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cidhna+Mine)
:    **[Damphall Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Damphall_Mine "Skyrim:Damphall Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small iron and silver mine north of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Damphall+Mine)
:   **[Dushnikh Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Mine "Skyrim:Dushnikh Mine")** — A small orichalcum mine supporting the Orc stronghold of Dushnikh Yal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Mine)
:    **[Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine")** — A small iron mine southwest of Riverwood containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Embershard+Mine)
:   **[Fenn's Gulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenn%27s_Gulch_Mine "Skyrim:Fenn's Gulch Mine")** — A small silver mine in northwestern Karthwasten. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fenn%27s+Gulch+Mine)
:    **[Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer")** — A medium-sized fort and iron mine south of Dawnstar containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Fellhammer)
:    **[Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine")** — A small ebony and iron mine supporting the Orc stronghold of Narzulbur. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gloombound+Mine)
:   **[Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine")** — A small corundum mine in southeastern Darkwater Crossing. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenrock+Mine)
:    **[Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp")** — A small bandit camp and iron mine north of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Halted+Stream+Camp)
:   **[Iron-Breaker Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron-Breaker_Mine "Skyrim:Iron-Breaker Mine")** — A small iron mine in eastern Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Iron-Breaker+Mine)
:    **[Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge")** — A small bandit camp and iron and corundum mine northwest of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Knifepoint+Ridge)
:    **[Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine")** — A small gold mine and settlement east-northeast of Markarth initially containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kolskeggr+Mine)
:    **[Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine")** — A small iron mine and settlement southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Left+Hand+Mine)
:    **[Lost Prospect Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Prospect_Mine "Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine")** — A small gold mine east-northeast of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Prospect+Mine)
:   **[Mor Khazgur Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Mine "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Mine")** — A small orichalcum mine supporting the Orc stronghold of Mor Khazgur. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur+Mine)
:    **[Northwind Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Mine "Skyrim:Northwind Mine")** — A small iron mine northwest of Shor's Stone containing skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Mine)
:   **[Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine")** — A small quicksilver mine in western Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Quicksilver+Mine)
:    **[Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small ebony mine in northern Raven Rock initially containing draugr, frostbite spiders, skeevers, and the dragon priest Zahkriisos. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Raven+Rock+Mine)
:   **[Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine")** — A small ebony mine in western Shor's Stone initially containing frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Redbelly+Mine)
:   **[Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine")** — A small iron mine in eastern Stonehills. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rockwallow+Mine)
:   **[Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine")** — A small silver mine in northern Karthwasten initially containing Silver-Blood mercenaries. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sanuarach+Mine)
:    **[Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole")** — A small moonstone mine and settlement east of Markarth initially containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Soljund%27s+Sinkhole)
:   **[Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine")** — A small malachite mine in northeastern Kynesgrove. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamscorch+Mine)
:    **[Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine")** — A small iron mine and settlement southeast of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Whistling+Mine)

# Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests/Ivarstead

## Overview

| Giver Location | Quest Giver | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Fellstar Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellstar_Farm "Skyrim:Fellstar Farm") | [Boti](/wiki/Skyrim:Boti "Skyrim:Boti") | **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Cabbage "Skyrim:Food"), [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Potato "Skyrim:Food"), [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") |  |  |

# Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests/Open World

## Overview

This page lists all of the **[Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests")** that are not confined to one location.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo") | [Khajiit Trade Caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") | **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) | - Find the Moon Amulet inside <Alias=Dungeon> - Return the Moon Amulet to Kharjo |  |

## Overview

This page lists all of the **[Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Solstheim "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests")** for the city of **[Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock")**.

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") | [The Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") | **[Feeding the Addiction](/wiki/Skyrim:Feeding_the_Addiction "Skyrim:Feeding the Addiction")**: Convince an [innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri") to let a [drunken miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel") get back to [the bar](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch"). | - Convince Geldis Sadri to admit Bralsa Drel to the inn - Tell Bralsa Drel she's welcome at the Retching Netch | [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") |

| [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") | [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei") | **[Sealing the Deal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealing_the_Deal "Skyrim:Sealing the Deal")**: Find three [flawless amethysts](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst") for [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei")'s engagement ring. | - Get 3 flawless amethysts for Talen-Jei - Return to Talen-Jei |  |
| [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") | [Galathil](/wiki/Skyrim:Galathil "Skyrim:Galathil") ([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) | **[Surgery](/wiki/Skyrim:Surgery "Skyrim:Surgery")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Change your appearance. ([DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")) *This quest does not count towards [Thane of the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift").* | - Locate the face sculptor in Riften - Talk to the face sculptor in the Ragged Flagon | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") installed |
| [The Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer") | [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund") | **[Stoking the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoking_the_Flames "Skyrim:Stoking the Flames")**: Find 10 [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") to restore [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund")'s forge. | - Bring 10 fire salts to Balimund - Return to Balimund |  |

# Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests

## Overview

**Miscellaneous quests** are minor quests. Completing objectives for miscellaneous quests increases the "Misc Objectives Completed" statistic in your journal and counts toward the [Hero of the People](#Achievements) [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements"). Miscellaneous quests are usually started and completed entirely within a single hold or area.

Miscellaneous quests are listed together in the "Miscellaneous" section in your journal. The actual name of each miscellaneous quest is not visible in game (the names used on this site are the names assigned to the quests in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit")). Only the current objective associated with each miscellaneous quest can be seen; completed objectives are not displayed, nor is any additional information about the current quest stage. Miscellaneous quests are different from [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests"), as the latter are full quests with complete entries in your journal.

Many miscellaneous quests use the [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quest system to add dynamic elements; therefore, details of the objectives for such quests (who assigns the quest, where to go, etc.) are likely to vary from one player to another. Radiant quests that can be obtained from multiple people are listed multiple times. Other radiant events you may encounter while exploring Skyrim for which no information is displayed in your journal are described separately on the [World Interactions](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") page.

This page **does not** list all of the miscellaneous quests available in the game. Faction-related miscellaneous quests, including those relevant to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"), [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Quests "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), as well as miscellaneous quests related to [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club_Quests "Skyrim:Creation Club Quests") content, are listed on their own pages. The three pages linked below include other miscellaneous quests which are not listed here:

- [Bounty Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_Quests "Skyrim:Bounty Quests")
- [Dungeon Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Quests#Dungeon_Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Dungeon Quests")
- [Tutorials](/wiki/Skyrim:Tutorials "Skyrim:Tutorials")

Most of the quests listed here are also [Favors](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") (highlighted in the tables below). Favors additionally include certain [Activities](/wiki/Skyrim:Activities "Skyrim:Activities") for which no information is displayed in your journal.

## Open World

| Quest Giver | Giver Location | Quest | Objective(s) | Requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)") | [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") | **[Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(quest) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (quest)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Learn a [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from [Durnehviir](/wiki/Skyrim:Durnehviir_(dragon) "Skyrim:Durnehviir (dragon)"). | - Speak to Durnehviir at his lair in the Soul Cairn - Summon Durnehviir in Tamriel - Learn the first word of Durnehviir's Shout - Learn the second word of Durnehviir's Shout - Learn the final word of Durnehviir's Shout | [Beyond Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Beyond_Death "Skyrim:Beyond Death") |
| [Soul](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul#xx002b0d "Skyrim:Soul") | [Soul Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn "Skyrim:Soul Cairn") | **[Soul Cairn Horse Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Cairn_Horse_Quest "Skyrim:Soul Cairn Horse Quest")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak")'s skull. | - Find Arvak's skull in the Soul Cairn - Retrieve Arvak's skull - Return Arvak's skull | [Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes") |

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is obtained by completing miscellaneous quests:

-  **Hero of the People** (30 points/Bronze) — Complete 50 Misc [Objectives](/wiki/Skyrim:Objectives "Skyrim:Objectives")
  - The game counts objectives completed, not quests completed; miscellaneous quests which have more than one objective count more heavily. It also counts all objectives completed, not just those that are part of the miscellaneous quests on this page. For example, if you join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") and get the objective "Talk to the Companions leaders for work", completing that objective counts toward the achievement.
  - The game also counts completing the same exact objective multiple times. For example, during the quest to retrieve 20 Deathbell, 20 Nightshade, and 20 Nirnroot for Ingun in Riften, every time you update your personal inventory from fewer than 20 to greater than or equal to 20 of any of the three ingredients, you will receive a quest objective update. You can therefore remain in a container menu and repeatedly shift these items back and forth in order to quickly unlock this achievement.
  - You can track your progress toward the achievement using the "Misc Objectives Completed" statistic on the "Quest" page of your journal's "General Stats".

## Notes

- Only one type of these miscellaneous quests can be active at a time:
  - **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Bugs

- Miscellaneous quests may disappear from your list of active quests, starting from the earliest quests forward. The quests are still active, however, and a quest will reappear if it is updated.
- Some radiant quests become unavailable if you do not receive them upon your first visit to the location, even if you avoid dialogue with the quest givers. This can be verified with Amren and Ysolda in Whiterun by riding to another city and back.

# Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests

## Overview

**Miscellaneous quests** are minor quests. Completing objectives for miscellaneous quests increases the "Misc Objectives Completed" statistic in your journal and counts toward the [Hero of the People](#Achievements) [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements"). Miscellaneous quests are usually started and completed entirely within a single hold or area.

Miscellaneous quests are listed together in the "Miscellaneous" section in your journal. The actual name of each miscellaneous quest is not visible in game (the names used on this site are the names assigned to the quests in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit")). Only the current objective associated with each miscellaneous quest can be seen; completed objectives are not displayed, nor is any additional information about the current quest stage. Miscellaneous quests are different from [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests"), as the latter are full quests with complete entries in your journal.

Many miscellaneous quests use the [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quest system to add dynamic elements; therefore, details of the objectives for such quests (who assigns the quest, where to go, etc.) are likely to vary from one player to another. Radiant quests that can be obtained from multiple people are listed multiple times. Other radiant events you may encounter while exploring Skyrim for which no information is displayed in your journal are described separately on the [World Interactions](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") page.

This page **does not** list all of the miscellaneous quests available in the game. Faction-related miscellaneous quests, including those relevant to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"), [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood#Quests "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), as well as miscellaneous quests related to [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club_Quests "Skyrim:Creation Club Quests") content, are listed on their own pages. The three pages linked below include other miscellaneous quests which are not listed here:

- [Bounty Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_Quests "Skyrim:Bounty Quests")
- [Dungeon Miscellaneous Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Quests#Dungeon_Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Dungeon Quests")
- [Tutorials](/wiki/Skyrim:Tutorials "Skyrim:Tutorials")

Most of the quests listed here are also [Favors](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") (highlighted in the tables below). Favors additionally include certain [Activities](/wiki/Skyrim:Activities "Skyrim:Activities") for which no information is displayed in your journal.

| [Morwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen "Skyrim:Morwen") | [Morwen's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen%27s_House "Skyrim:Morwen's House") | **[Skaal Village Dialogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village_Dialogue "Skyrim:Skaal Village Dialogue")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Take [Bera's necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Bera%27s_Necklace "Skyrim:Bera's Necklace") to [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). | - Take Bera's Necklace to Runil in Falkreath - Return to Morwen in Skaal Village | [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal") |

[†](#note_Stalhrim)Only the first part of this quest is classed as miscellaneous, but both are documented on the same page.

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is obtained by completing miscellaneous quests:

-  **Hero of the People** (30 points/Bronze) — Complete 50 Misc [Objectives](/wiki/Skyrim:Objectives "Skyrim:Objectives")
  - The game counts objectives completed, not quests completed; miscellaneous quests which have more than one objective count more heavily. It also counts all objectives completed, not just those that are part of the miscellaneous quests on this page. For example, if you join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") and get the objective "Talk to the Companions leaders for work", completing that objective counts toward the achievement.
  - The game also counts completing the same exact objective multiple times. For example, during the quest to retrieve 20 Deathbell, 20 Nightshade, and 20 Nirnroot for Ingun in Riften, every time you update your personal inventory from fewer than 20 to greater than or equal to 20 of any of the three ingredients, you will receive a quest objective update. You can therefore remain in a container menu and repeatedly shift these items back and forth in order to quickly unlock this achievement.
  - You can track your progress toward the achievement using the "Misc Objectives Completed" statistic on the "Quest" page of your journal's "General Stats".

## Notes

- Only one type of these miscellaneous quests can be active at a time:
  - **[A Few Words with You](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You "Skyrim:A Few Words with You")**: Do a favor by talking to someone about a problem. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
  - **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Bugs

- Miscellaneous quests may disappear from your list of active quests, starting from the earliest quests forward. The quests are still active, however, and a quest will reappear if it is updated.
- Some radiant quests become unavailable if you do not receive them upon your first visit to the location, even if you avoid dialogue with the quest givers. This can be verified with Amren and Ysolda in Whiterun by riding to another city and back.

# Skyrim:Missing In Action

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. | **Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
