| ID: | MS09 |
| Suggested Level: | 12 |

Avulstein attempts a rescue mission

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Learn of the ongoing feud in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
2. Talk to [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane") or [Avulstein Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Avulstein_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Avulstein Gray-Mane").
3. Find a revealing [missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Missive_(Battle-Born) "Skyrim:Imperial Missive (Battle-Born)") in the Battle-Born house.
4. *Optional:* Recruit Avulstein Gray-Mane as a follower.
5. Journey to [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep") and rescue [Thorald](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from his [abductors](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
6. Return to [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane") for your reward.

### An Ongoing Feud

A confrontation in the streets

While in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), you will likely overhear an argument between [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane") and two Battle-Borns, [Idolaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born") and [Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born"), by her stall in the market.

:   **Olfrid**: *"Foolish old woman! You know nothing! Nothing of our struggles, our suffering!"*
:   **Fralia**: *"Nothing? And what of my son? Hmm? What of [Thorald](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane")? Is he nothing? So don't talk to me about suffering!"*
:   **Idolaf**: *"Your son chose his side, and he chose poorly. And now he's gone. Such is the way of war. The sooner you accept his loss, the better."*
:   **Fralia**: *"I will never accept his death! My son still lives. I feel it in my heart. So tell me, Battle-Borns, where is he? Where are you holding my Thorald?"*
:   **Olfrid**: *"Do you believe this old hag? "Holding him"? Why I've got him in my cellar. He's my prisoner. Face it, cow! Your stupid son is dead! He died a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") traitor. And you... you best keep your mouth shut before you suffer the same."*
:   **Idolaf**: *"Come on, father. There's nothing more to be said here."*

If you talk to Idolaf or Olfrid about the argument they will explain about how the Battle-Borns and Gray-Manes had been friends once, but because of the ongoing [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") the families have had a falling out due to them taking opposing sides. After the argument is over proceed to talk to Fralia; she will say that [Thorald](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") isn't dead and when asked how she can be so sure of that fact will comment that it isn't safe to talk there and will ask you to meet her in her house later if you want to help.

#### House Gray-Mane

Avulstein Gray-Mane

Head up the hill and enter [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane") where an armed man will rush at you, but Fralia calls out for him to stop; he is her son, [Avulstein Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Avulstein_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Avulstein Gray-Mane"), who has been hiding in the house for fear of being arrested by the Imperials if discovered. He tells you more of the story and what he wants done: *"I know that Thorald's not dead. I just know it. The [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") have him, and are keeping him somewhere. But I don't know where. Those damned Battle-Borns... they know something. They're hiding it. They practically taunt us with it. They must have some sort of proof! There's got to be something in that house of theirs. I just know it. I don't dare leave the house myself. So I need your help."*

### Missing In Action

The Battle-Borns' secret

To find out what really happened to Thorald, you'll need to get your hands on an [imperial missive](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Missive_(Battle-Born) "Skyrim:Imperial Missive (Battle-Born)") in the possession of the Battle-Borns. There are three alternative ways to do so, each of which leverages a [stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") skill: [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking"), [Pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") and [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech").

- **Lockpicking method**: You have to trespass in the [Battle-Borns' house](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born") to retrieve the missive. It is located on the ground floor in a small office adjoining a bedroom; it is on the left from the front door. The office door is locked and there is no key for it; the key that can be pickpocketed from Battle-Born family members only opens the exterior doors. To simplify the task you can gain free access to the house by raising a resident's disposition, for example by helping [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born") with his [bullying problem](/wiki/Skyrim:Bullying_Braith "Skyrim:Bullying Braith"), answering "Battle-Born" to your Idolaf's first ever greeting or by [selling crops](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") to [Alfhild Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Alfhild_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Alfhild Battle-Born"). The lock to the office door must be picked anyway, although sometimes a Battle-Born will have been in that room and left the door wide open.
- **Pickpocket method**: [Jon Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Jon_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Jon Battle-Born") carries a [love letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Olfina "Skyrim:Letter from Olfina") from [Olfina Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane"). Pickpocket it from him, then talk to him about Thorald. He'll initially refuse to say much, but with the letter you can blackmail him into retrieving the missive and meeting you at the Talos statue to hand it over to you.
- **Speech method**: The quickest way is to pass a hard [persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuade "Skyrim:Persuade") check ([Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") level 75) with [Idolaf Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born"). He'll tell you that the Gray-Manes are better off believing Thorald to be dead than knowing the truth. He once tried to look into the situation through his Legion contacts, as Thorald was once his friend, but was cut short. However he managed to find out that the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") detain him at [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep"), a place people don't ever come back from. He will finally give you the missive as proof of his story.

With the missive in your hands you may return to the Gray-Manes' to share what you discovered. If the door is locked, wait until [Eorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") returns home at 9pm. Once you're inside, speak with [Avulstein](/wiki/Skyrim:Avulstein_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Avulstein Gray-Mane"), who will propose to round up some men ([Geirlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirlund "Skyrim:Geirlund") and [Vidrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vidrald "Skyrim:Vidrald")) to assault the fortress; you can agree to meet him there or tell him to stay put and let you handle it yourself. After making your decision, it's on to Northwatch Keep.

### Prisoner of War

Northwatch Keep is occupied by [Thalmor Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Generic_Thalmor_NPCs "Skyrim:Thalmor"), who will all turn hostile if you ignore the warnings to stay away. If you talk to the [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Guard "Skyrim:Northwatch Guard") at the front entrance, you will have an option to ask for the release of Thorald. The guard will respond with, *"Are you joking? Even if we had a prisoner by that name, the only way he'd be released is by order of the Imperial Legion."* You can travel to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and talk to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"), who will deny the request: *"The Thalmor? Do you have any idea what you're asking? I'm sorry, that's just not possible. It would cause far too many problems."* The peaceful method of solving the quest is [incomplete](#Bugs), however, and cannot be pursued further. Once the diplomatic approach fails, return to Northwatch Keep and consider your remaining options.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Avoid the patrols  **Stealth** To sneak in, enter the grounds through the back gate in the northeast section of the compound, then look to the right and pick the master-level door. Once inside, head down the stairs. Around the corner is a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Thalmor_Soldiers "Skyrim:Thalmor") and an [archer](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Archer "Skyrim:Northwatch Archer"); one is patrolling while the other is sitting at a small table. They must be killed to safely escort Thorald out, and if you can do so quickly and quietly you should be able to prevent the guard in the next room from responding. Moving past the next guard and into the far room you will find the [Northwatch Interrogator](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Interrogator "Skyrim:Northwatch Interrogator"), who must also be killed to safely release Thorald. You won't need his [Northwatch Keep key](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep_Key "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep Key") since you already unlocked the back door, but be sure to help yourself to the contents of the treasure chest. Speak to Thorald and he will be released from his shackles after a few moments to follow you, stopping to pick up a weapon along the way. Even though Thorald does not sneak, you can still slip by the previous guard who should still be oblivious to the jail break if you haven't made a lot of noise. | The garrison  **Assault** This is definitely the more profitable method, as the Thalmor soldiers at Northwatch will be equipped with leveled (steel, elven, glass) weapons and armor. If you opted to bring Avulstein with you, it is likely that Vidrald will die, and Geirlund is level 1 and essentially doomed. They wear leveled heavy and light armor respectively and carry leveled weapons. The haul taken from the dead Thalmor troops will be worth far more than your actual reward, and there's so much good loot available that you may wish to bring a follower to help you carry it all even if that's not normally your style. If you chose to let Avulstein come, then he and two mercenaries will be waiting for you behind some rocks near the fort; go talk to him and they'll begin their attack. There are four Northwatch guards patrolling the grounds and three Northwatch archers patrolling the walkways above who will all turn hostile when you enter the grounds. The fort is pretty straightforward once you're inside; just press on ahead and kill every elf in sight. You'll pass through a mess hall with a bar where you can find a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")*, and further on down in a small room on the bottom floor of a big room you can find a Thalmor mage carrying the [Northwatch captain's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Captain%27s_Key "Skyrim:Northwatch Captain's Key") and the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[The Legendary Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legendary_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:The Legendary Sancre Tor")*. As usual, keep an eye out for treasure chests along the way. |

#### The Interrogator

The Northwatch Interrogator

Near the end of the dungeon you'll reach a T-shaped intersection; to the left is the interrogation chamber where Thorald is being held, to the right is a cell block beyond which is the exit door. There are also racks of weapons in this area. Head left and kill the interrogator if you haven't done so already to get the Northwatch Keep key, then loot the big treasure chest and free Thorald. Lead him up through the cell blocks to the exit (you can release the [prisoners](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Prisoner "Skyrim:Northwatch Prisoner") here but they won't actually leave, though they will fight the Thalmor next door causing a distraction) and use the interrogator's key to unlock the door.

### Freedom!

Gray-Manes Reunited

Once outside in a safe location, Thorald will thank you for releasing him, saying *"I cannot thank you enough for rescuing me from this place. I suspect I'd never again see the light of day otherwise. But why would you risk your life for me, a stranger?"* Once the details are explained he will ask you to get word to his mother and will give you a message that she should recognize. He'll then leave to join the Stormcloaks, as he doesn't feel safe in Whiterun anymore. If Avulstein is with you, they'll exchange a few words and he'll agree to follow Thorald; if not then Thorald will tell you that Avulstein should leave Whiterun too as the Thalmor will surely come looking for him (in which case Avulstein will already be gone by the time you get back to Whiterun).

Return to Fralia and she'll ask you where Thorald is. After you tell her that he's not coming, she'll say *"What? After all this, I can't even see him? How... How do I know you're telling me the truth, and not just what I want to hear?"*, giving you a chance to use the secret message **"suffer the winter's cold wind..."**, which she completes: *"...for it bears aloft next summer's seeds." That's my boy. So it's true, then. For now, it's enough to know that he's alive. I can find peace in that. Thank you, dear friend. You've given me back my son."* She'll then reward you with an enchanted weapon that Eorlund had made for Thorald. In the case that Eorlund is dead, she will instead give you 200 gold as a reward.

## Notes

- The quest can be started by entering the Gray-Manes' home and talking to Avulstein, skipping the conversations with Fralia.
- This quest counts towards the [Sideways](/wiki/Skyrim:Sideways "Skyrim:Sideways") [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") regardless of how you choose to complete it (i.e., both quest stages 200 and 201 qualify).
- While Thorald and his family are aligned with the Stormcloaks, an Imperial-aligned character can complete this quest without additional difficulty.
- If you find Thorald before the relevant stage of the quest, he will simply say *"You there! What are you doing?"* and you will not be able to release him.
- Even if Whiterun is under Stormcloak control, Thorald and Avulstein will still believe that it is not safe for them there.
- Avulstein will always be disabled from the game once you return to Fralia after Thorald has been rescued, regardless of which path you choose.
- If you follow Thorald after rescuing him, you will find that he will travel to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") in Windhelm, although there is no further interaction between Thorald and the other Stormcloaks.
- If Northwatch Keep has been cleared before and the peaceful path is chosen, then the guards will not respawn and thus the peaceful path will automatically fail upon arrival at Northwatch Keep. There is however a way to go onto the peaceful way using console commands. First, add yourself to the Thalmor faction using the command `player.addfac 00039f26 0`, then spawn in a Northwatch Guard to trigger dialogue using `player.placeatme 000C07C2`. You will then be able to continue as if you had never wiped Northwatch Keep before.
- Geirlund, unlike Vidrald, is not a leveled actor and will almost certainly die if he accompanies you.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- Jon Battle-Born never takes Olfina's letter back if you pickpocket it from him as a way to get the evidence.
- If you try to rescue Thorald in werewolf form, he will free himself and become hostile.

## Bugs

- The peaceful method of completing the quest is incomplete. The [Imperial Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Order "Skyrim:Imperial Order") for Thorald's release was not finished and Tullius will simply deny the request. However, there is dialogue for granting the request (*"I can only imagine the headaches this is going to cause... Here, take this. Assuming they even honor it, you should be able to get your prisoner out."*), that was supposed to trigger if you have completed the Imperial Legion questline. The faulty parameters for the dialogue are that you need to be above or equal to rank 0 in the Imperial Legion faction, but also that the denial dialogue (which takes priority) requires you to be below rank 5 in the faction.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. To obtain the order you must side with the Imperial Legion in the civil war questline and then speak to General Tullius. When you get to Northwatch, give the guard the orders and he will walk you to the prisoner. Once you've spoken to Thorald, the quest continues as normal. However, Thorald will not return to his family in Whiterun and will still have the same dialogue telling he is not safe in Whiterun and must fall in with the ranks of the Stormcloaks, even if you release him using this peaceful method after the Civil War is completed.
- After completing the quest, [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep") remains uninhabited. If either of or both [Geirlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirlund "Skyrim:Geirlund") and [Vidrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Vidrald "Skyrim:Vidrald") manage to survive (given you asked them for help), they will remain outside the keep, but they will not have any unique dialogue when spoken to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- Fralia's dialogue at the beginning of the quest may occur without either of the Battle-Borns being present.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If you wait too long to meet her Fralia at her home after speaking to her in the market, she will not speak to you there, instead remaining stuck at the market waiting for you to talk to her. The quest will not progress at this point.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- Upon retrieving the missive and attempting to present it to Avulstein, the Gray-Mane home may be permanently locked. This may also happen before meeting Fralia in her house, and it may be caused by waiting for too long between assignments. Sneaking in, even with a pickpocketed key, will make Avulstein and Fralia hostile, telling you that you're not supposed to be there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=17127))
  -  To fix this, use the pair of console commands `Prid 1A686` and `moveto player` in succession to make Avulstein spawn at your location. You can then talk to him outside the house, where he won't be hostile.
  - If it happens before meeting Fralia in the house, you may need to advance the stage using console because she will not speak to you outside. To fix this type on console: `movetoqt MS09` and you will be put inside the Gray-Mane household.
  - The easiest way to fix this is first running away from him until he loses track of you and then either sleep in the bed available not far to the west or to fast travel from the location and then back again.
- If you rescue Thorald without presenting the proof to Avulstein, the quest marker for him will point to a disabled NPC. Nevertheless, you can still complete the quest by heading straight to Fralia.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19993))
- Jon Battle-Born never takes back Olfina's letter to him if you pickpocketed it from him as a way to get the evidence.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.
- This quest may set off trespass warnings when entering Fralia's house.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. A trigger box outside the home has been added which will enable the public flag on the cell and unlock both entrance doors so you don't have to pick either one.
- The Thalmor inside the keep may turn hostile even with the release order.
  -  It is possible to go through, type `player.addfac 00039F26 0` using the console to temporarily add yourself to their faction. Once you have freed the prisoner and are out of reach, type `player.addfac 00039F26 -1` to remove yourself from the Thalmor faction.
  -  An alternative solution if the `player.addfac 0009F26 0` command above doesn't work can be achieved by selecting a Thalmor soldier and typing `setav aggression 0` in the console, although this solution can be time consuming if the player wishes to remove the aggression factor from every single Thalmor soldier.
- Thorald may just stand where he was released with his brother and they will not follow you.
  - Thorald can be forced into action by "pushing" him (walking, running, or rolling into him until he moves) away from the dungeon and down the hall toward the next room. Eventually he will begin to run on his own.
  - Thorald was scripted to pick up a weapon as soon as he is free before following you out which may be the reason for his static behavior. Dropping a weapon near him may result in him picking it up and being ready to move. The weapon cannot be marked "stolen".
  -  Players on PC may force-equip Thorald with a weapon in the console, by activating the console key then clicking on him and typing (for example) `equipitem 13983 1`.
- Thorald may just stand at door and not run away after exiting the building.
  - Once any nearby enemies are dealt with, talk to him to advance the quest.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MS09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS09`.

# Skyrim:Missing Merchant

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **A powerful set of armor has come on the market.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | The innkeeper of [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") ([Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn") or [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils")) |
| Location(s): | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post") |
| Reward: | [Daedric mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Daedric Mail") set, optionally [Ring of Masser](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Masser "Skyrim:Ring of Masser") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE051\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail") |

An incriminating scene

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to an innkeeper or wait for a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier").
2. Kill [Erwan](/wiki/Skyrim:Erwan "Skyrim:Erwan") at [Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post") and obtain *[Erwan's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Erwan%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Erwan's Journal")* and the [Ring of Masser](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Masser "Skyrim:Ring of Masser").
3. Obtain the set of [Daedric mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Daedric Mail") armor from [Ma'dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27dran "Skyrim:Ma'dran").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to an innkeeper and ask them for work. You will be handed a note titled *[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant_(note) "Skyrim:Missing Merchant (note)")* and the quest begins.

You learn that the jarl has put out a call for aid regarding the disappearance of a merchant, [Gunther Frost-Foot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunther "Skyrim:Gunther"), who was last seen in the area of [Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post") east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). You will be tasked to go there and investigate.

Traitor's Post, a destroyed cabin, is currently home to a gang of bandits led by a Breton female named [Erwan](/wiki/Skyrim:Erwan "Skyrim:Erwan"). Upon killing Erwan, you will be prompted to loot her body and read her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Erwan%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Erwan's Journal"). Erwan, it seems, is quite disturbed, and currently considers the corpse of Gunther to be her "best friend". She mentions in passing that she sold a suit of [Daedric mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Daedric Mail") to a Khajiit caravaner named [Ma'dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27dran "Skyrim:Ma'dran"), but that he should be willing to trade the armor for a ring she currently possesses. This ring is the [Ring of Masser](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Masser "Skyrim:Ring of Masser"), which you will find on Gunther's naked corpse within the cabin.

You will be prompted to track down Ma'dran, whose [trade caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") travels between Windhelm and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). You then have the choice of either trading the ring to him for a set of [Daedric mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Daedric Mail") armor, or paying 5,000 gold for the armor. The ring has a base value of 5,211, so this is a fair trade if you don't wish to keep it. The quest will complete once you have obtained the set of armor, and you will subsequently begin to find Daedric mail items as random loot throughout the world.

## Notes

- Regular Daedric armor starts appearing in leveled lists at level 48, but this Creation is not level-locked and can be completed by characters of any level.
  - Paired with [the Bittercup creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup") and specifically choosing [to fill the Altar of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pit_(quest) "Skyrim:The Pit (quest)"), you can get a full set of Daedric armor at level one, with both normal and mail gauntlets.

Mistveil Keep in Riften

**Mistveil Keep** is a castle located at the southern end of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Its grand stone walls stand out from Riften's wooden buildings and walkways, and also serve as an extra layer of protection in times of conflict.

There are three zones to the keep: *[Mistveil Keep](#Mistveil_Keep)*, *[Mistveil Keep Barracks](#Mistveil_Keep_Barracks)*, and *[Mistveil Keep Jarl's Chambers](#Mistveil_Keep_Jarl.27s_Chambers)*. The building also encompasses [Riften Jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Jail "Skyrim:Riften Jail"), though it is a separate place. There is a small [courtyard](#Courtyard) beside the building.

The Keep is home to Jarl [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver"), and her sons, [Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald") and [Saerlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Saerlund "Skyrim:Saerlund"). As the seat of power, the hold's [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward"), [Anuriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel"), and [court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Court_Wizard "Skyrim:Court Wizard"), [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah"), can be found here.

## NPCs Living Here

## Related Quests

- **[Bring It!](/wiki/Skyrim:Bring_It! "Skyrim:Bring It!")**: Deliver [Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald")'s sword.
- **[Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)")**: Use a [corrupt steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Anuriel "Skyrim:Anuriel") to gain intelligence on the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Hunt and Gather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunt_and_Gather "Skyrim:Hunt and Gather")**: Retrieve [Wylandriah](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah "Skyrim:Wylandriah")'s [spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Spoon "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Spoon"), [ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Orichalcum_Ingot "Skyrim:Quest Items"), and [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Wylandriah%27s_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Wylandriah's Soul Gem").
- **[I Done Got Thaned!](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!")**: Help out the Jarl and citizens of the Rift, and be named Thane for your service. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[The Raid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Raid "Skyrim:The Raid")**: Help the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") to uncover and stop the illegal [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") trade in town.
  - **[Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")**: Clear [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Courtyard

The courtyard is to the left of the building. It is used as a dining and training area by the guards, and also has a direct entrance to the [keep's barracks](#Mistveil_Keep_Barracks). There is a [walkway](#Walkway) above the courtyard, underneath which is a long table with two benches and two chairs, and a few barrels. The door to the barracks is to the south, and to the right of it is a [chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). Around the rest of the courtyard can be found three training dummies. Harrald likes to train here during the day.

### Mistveil Keep

The first room of Mistveil Keep is both a dining room and a throne room. To the left is a door to [Wylandriah's shop](#Wylandriah.27s_Shop), and behind the throne is a corridor leading to [Anuriel's bedroom](#Anuriel.27s_bedroom), the *[Mistveil Keep Jarl's Chambers](#Mistveil_Keep_Jarl.27s_Chambers)*, the [war room](#War_Room), [Unmid Snow-Shod's bedroom](#Unmid_Snow-Shod.27s_bedroom), and the *[Mistveil Keep Barracks](#Mistveil_Keep_Barracks)*. The jarl's chambers and the barracks have individual zones while the rest are in the Mistveil Keep zone.

Throne Room

The throne room/dining room is rather cramped with all the furniture in it. There is a small fire in the middle of the lower area with three long tables set in a U around it. Past the tables, on a raised section is the throne, beside which is a chair for the hold's steward. Around the edges of the room are some more pieces of furniture set out almost symmetrically. From the entrance there are two benches, a set of shelves, a small table with a platter of food, a long chest, another set of shelves, and finally another bench. The only difference between the sides of the room is on the left, where the small table is removed, with the set of shelves moving to its location, and a door to Wylandriah's shop.

Wylandriah's Shop

Wylandriah's shop is subdivided into two rooms, her shop and her bedroom. The shop counter is on the other side of the room, and a bit to the left. Beside it is a set of shelves with some ingredients. In the corners of the room to the left is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). The bedroom is to the right from the counter and contains only a few items of furniture (a bed, a chest, a wardrobe, an end table, and a chair).

On the shop counter is a mix of weapons, armor, potions, and ingredients; they include a [hide shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield"), a [hide helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"), a [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), a [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), a [spider egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), and two [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"). Underneath the counter is a medium coin purse and a letter entitled '[Per Your Requests](/wiki/Skyrim:Per_Your_Requests "Skyrim:Per Your Requests")'. On the set of shelves by the counter are three bowls of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a bowl of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), two samples of [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), and two samples of scaly pholiota.

Anuriel's Bedroom

Anuriel's bedroom is to the right along the corridor behind the throne. Along the section of corridor to it is a table with the book *[Short History of Morrowind](/wiki/Skyrim:Short_History_of_Morrowind "Skyrim:Short History of Morrowind")* on it. The room contains a cupboard, a wardrobe, a chest, a double-bed, an end table, and a dresser. On the cupboard is a note entitled '[Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar_(note) "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar (note)")', on the end table is a copy of the book *[The Dowry](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dowry "Skyrim:The Dowry")*, and on the dresser is an adept-locked display case, a copy of *[A Dance in Fire, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v5 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v5")*, a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"). The display case holds a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace"), and a [silver sapphire necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Sapphire_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Sapphire Necklace"), and there is a large coin purse to the right behind the dresser. There is also a table at the end of the bed holding a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), a lavender, and a bowl of apples.

War Room

The war room is to the left along the corridor behind the throne. The main focus of the room is a map with markers for all the important strategic points in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). There is also a cupboard, a set of shelves, and a table. There are also doors to the [Unmid Snow-Shod's bedroom](#Unmid_Snow-Shod.27s_bedroom), and the *[Mistveil Keep Barracks](#Mistveil_Keep_Barracks)*. [Gonnar Oath-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Gonnar_Oath-Giver "Skyrim:Gonnar Oath-Giver") spends his days here, studying the map.

Unmid Snow-Shod's Bedroom

Unmid Snow-Shod's bedroom is located to the south of the war room. It contains a weapon rack, a dresser, a wardrobe, a chest, a bed, an end table, a display case, a weapon plaque, and a training dummy. There is an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") on the weapon rack, and a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") on the weapon plaque. The display case has an adept lock and contains a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and [steel imperial gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Imperial Gauntlets").

## Mistveil Keep Barracks

There are two entrances to the barracks, one in the [courtyard](#Courtyard), and one in the [war room](#War_Room) inside the keep. There is another door inside the barracks that leads to a short [walkway](#Walkway) above the courtyard. There are two floors to the barracks: the [lower floor](#Lower_Floor) which has a few beds and a kitchen, and the [upper floor](#Upper_Floor) which has more beds, some storage space, and a small armory.

Lower Floor

From the door to the keep there are two beds on both sides, each accompanied by a chest. Above the two left-hand beds are two weapon plaques, each with a steel sword. After the beds there is a table with three chairs and some food to the left and the stairs to the upper floor on the right. To the left of the stairs is a small storage area with some straw bales, boxes, barrels, and a [pitchfork](/wiki/Skyrim:Pitchfork "Skyrim:Pitchfork"). After the table to the left is a door to the [courtyard](#Courtyard) and the kitchen area. Opposite the door is a dresser, beside which a guard stands. The kitchen area is made up of a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), a set of shelves with cutlery and pots, another set of shelves with food, a long table with a bench with some food on the table, and a round table with three chairs. Above the food shelves some ingredients are growing, two [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a [garlic bud](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic").

Upper Floor

The upper floor is divided into more private sections with wooden partitions. On the right at the top of the stairs is a storage area with two barrels. After that is an end table with a keg and opposite that is a section with two beds, each with a chest, and between them another end table with a copy of the book *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*. To the left of that section is another bed, with an end table beside it with a copy of the book *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*. To the left of the stairway is another partitioned section with two beds, each with a chest, and an end table in-between. The final partitioned section, in the southwest corner of the room, has a bed, an end table, and a dresser. On the end table is a loaf of bread, and on the dresser is an iron greatsword and a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*. Beside that section is a small selection of arms, divided between a locked display case and a weapon rack. The display case holds an iron and a steel mace, and the weapon rack holds two iron maces, an iron sword, an iron warhammer, and an iron battleaxe. Finally, before the door to the walkway in the northeast corner, is a table with two chairs and some food, beside some storage containers.

#### Riften

The walkway is L-shaped and spans the length of the courtyard. There is nothing besides three barrels on it (one of which is a thieves cache).

## Mistveil Keep Jarl's Chambers

The chambers are located on the upper floors of the keep. The stairs to the chambers are located to the right, along the corridor behind the throne. They are locked at night when the jarl goes to bed, but unlocked during the day. Through the door is a flight of stairs leading to a landing with three additional doors. They lead to [Saerlund's bedroom](#Saerlund.27s_Bedroom) on the left, the [jarl's bedroom](#Jarl.27s_Bedroom) straight ahead, and [Harrald's bedroom](#Harrald.27s_Bedroom) on the right.

Jarl's Bedroom

The jarl's bedroom is the largest of the three upstairs rooms; in fact it is more than twice the size of the other two combined. There is also a small storage area partially split off, and a door to an outer [balcony](#Balcony) that overlooks Riften. The room can be considered to be divided into two halves. The side on the right is for relaxing and eating, and the side on the left is the actual bed, with assorted accessories.

There is a long chest at the bottom of the bed, a small and a large wardrobe, and an end table to the left of the bed, and an end table, a large wardrobe, and a locked display case to the right of the bed. On top of the end table to the left is an [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), and a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill book *[Surfeit of Thieves](/wiki/Skyrim:Surfeit_of_Thieves "Skyrim:Surfeit of Thieves")*. In a bowl on top of the small wardrobe are two samples of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). The display case holds a [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet"), a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield"), and some [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"). Above the display case is a weapon plaque with an elven greatsword.

The other side of the room has a fireplace with two chairs and a small table in front of it. To the right of the fireplace are sets of shelves and a bench, and on the left-hand side are two more benches and a table. On the shelves are two potions (a [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration") and a [Draught of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength")), a sample of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), and two samples of lavender.

There are two sides to the small storage area on the other side of the bedroom. To the left are two barrels, some boxes, and a shelf with some wine. To the right is a barrel, some sacks, and some shelves filled with food and potions. There are four potions in total: two potions of minor stamina, and two potions of minor healing.

Saerlund's Bedroom

Saerlund's bedroom is to the left at the top of the stairs. It contains a long chest, a wardrobe, an end table, a bed, another end table, another wardrobe, and a table with two chairs. On top of the first wardrobe is a locked display case which contains an iron dagger. There is a lute by the second wardrobe, and some food on the table.

Harrald's Bedroom

Harrald's bedroom is to the right at the top of the stairs. It contains a chest, two wardrobes, a bed, an end table, a small table and chair, and a set of shelves. On top of the small wardrobe is a locked display case which contains an Orcish dagger and a steel dagger. On the table there is a salmon steak, some baked potatoes, and a loaf of bread. There are six books on the shelves; there are copies of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, *[Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Harvesting_Frostbite_Spider_Venom "Skyrim:Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom")*, *[Herbane's Bestiary: Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Hagravens "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Hagravens")*, *[Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Ice_Wraiths "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Ice Wraiths")*, *[Ode To The Tundrastriders](/wiki/Skyrim:Ode_To_The_Tundrastriders "Skyrim:Ode To The Tundrastriders")*, and *[Troll Slaying](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Slaying "Skyrim:Troll Slaying")*. Behind the door is an inaccessible weapon plaque with iron greatsword.

#### Riften

Through the jarl's bedroom is a door to a balcony that overlooks Riften. It is devoid of furniture and items. It has a low-hanging wooden roof that allows you to see out, but there is not enough room to get out between the wall and the ceiling.

## Notes

- If the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") gains control of the Rift, [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") will become the jarl, with her son [Hemming](/wiki/Skyrim:Hemming_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Hemming Black-Briar") as her steward and [Maul](/wiki/Skyrim:Maul "Skyrim:Maul") as her housecarl. Laila Law-Giver, Anuriel, and Unmid Snow-Shod will be exiled to Windhelm's [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings").

# Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") |
| Location(s): | [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") |
| Reward: | [Fjola's Wedding Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola%27s_Wedding_Band "Skyrim:Fjola's Wedding Band") |
| ID: | dunMistwatchQST |
| Required Items: | [Mistwatch Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Key "Skyrim:Mistwatch Key"), [Fjola's Wedding Band](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola%27s_Wedding_Band "Skyrim:Fjola's Wedding Band") |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| Difficulty: | Easy |

A view of a dragon flying above Mistwatch

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") and deal with the [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") outside.
2. Drop the drawbridge and enter Mistwatch North Tower.
3. Speak to [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") and agree to help him find his kidnapped [wife](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").
4. Proceed through the tower to the Mistwatch Lower Balcony.
5. Enter the Mistwatch West Tower.
6. Proceed through the tower to the Mistwatch Upper Balcony.
7. Enter the Mistwatch East Tower.
8. Deal with the bandit leader.
9. Return to Christer.

### North Mistwatch Tower

Drawbridge lever to access the Northern Tower.

Once you have breached the outer region of Mistwatch, find a lever located on the first level above ground. This will lower the bridge to enter the North tower. Once inside you will encounter a Nord named [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer"). Speaking with him and accepting his request will initiate the quest. Entering the North Tower through any other entrance makes [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") inaccessible, as the room he is in requires the key he is holding to enter from the other side (see Notes at the end of the page for details). As you speak to him he will tell you that his wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola") is missing and believes she is being held here. According to his story the [Mistwatch bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") started kidnapping and ransoming people around the time of her disappearance. He has managed to sneak in past the initial guards in the courtyard, but can't make it any further. That he hasn't been contacted by the bandits despite their ransom motives foreshadows a situation in which you will have to make a difficult decision should you choose to accept his quest. If you accept he will provide the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Key "Skyrim:Mistwatch Key") that is needed to unlock the gate leading to the rest of the tower. Past the locked door will be two leveled bandits and the ladder exit to the lower balcony.

### West Mistwatch Tower

Trap door access to Mistwatch from the cliffs above.

The West Mistwatch Tower has four leveled bandits who will ambush you immediately upon entry. There is a chest to the left of the first unlocked cell containing a dead [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)"), but this isn't Fjola. A [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_(Mistwatch) "Skyrim:Note (Mistwatch)") on the table next to the cell provides some insight into the situation. There are two bottles of Ale next to a lantern with a Long Taffy Treat on one table. You will find several beds scattered throughout the lower tier of the tower, as well as one more table with two bottles of Ale but nothing more of interest.
Moving up the first flight of stairs you will encounter a table with a quiver of Dwarven Arrows next to a few drums and some food items. A final table with a kettle and an iron dagger marks the entry way to the Higher Balcony.

### East Mistwatch Tower

The bandit leader approaches.

The East Mistwatch Tower is through the upper balcony. Unlocking its door requires the Mistwatch Key given to you by Christer. Inside is a single room and only one person—a [Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). Instead of attacking, she will start talking to you, revealing that she is in fact Fjola. She was never kidnapped and the kidnappings only started happening after she disappeared because they were her idea. She will explain that she couldn't take her life anymore and quickly joined and whipped these bandits into shape when she returned to [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). She still holds some sort of love for Christer and doesn't want him harmed, but doesn't want him in her life anymore. You will be presented with two options. Don't forget to pick up a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")* from Fjola's dresser in her sleeping quarters, located just beyond where she approaches you in the east tower before leaving to make your decision.

#### Kill the Bandit Leader

One choice is to kill Fjola. You don't even have to hear Fjola's story. By killing her you are left with only a hint of her true identity given by [the wedding band](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola%27s_Wedding_Band "Skyrim:Fjola's Wedding Band") found on her corpse. At this point you need to return to [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") and tell him the bad news. If you do this, your only option will be to tell him that you killed Fjola because she attacked you, in which case he will become enraged and attempt to take revenge for her death.

It is possible to yield to Christer once he attacks, and he then becomes non-hostile again, and you then have the conversation options as if you were tricking him.

#### Trick Christer into Leaving

The other choice is to agree to lie to Christer and get him to leave. Fjola gives you her wedding band as proof to present to Christer and tells you to keep it once he has left. You can tell Christer either that Fjola is dead or you only found her ring. Either way he is relieved, gives the ring back to you as reward, and takes off to start living again.

You can complete the quest by telling Fjola that you have convinced Christer to leave — which only requires going a short distance up the stairs, because Fjola has followed you down into North Mistwatch Tower. She'll promise to return the favor one day in the future and the quest will end (including marking Mistwatch as cleared on your map).

## Notes

- If Christer dies at any point before the quest is completed, it becomes impossible to finish the quest.
- If you drop down onto the roof of Mistwatch from the mountains at the rear, and work down through the towers instead of up, you cannot open the final door before reaching Christer, because the Mistwatch key can only be obtained from Christer. To proceed, you will need to go back out through the trapdoor at the top of the North Tower, jump down, and re-enter the North Tower through the main door. With the key you will then be able to go back up and enter the East Mistwatch Tower to complete the quest.
  - It is possible to obtain a copy of the Mistwatch key without speaking to Christer if you have the  [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking#Skill_Perks "Skyrim:Lockpicking") perk and unlock any of the master-locked entrances. After obtaining the key, if you speak to Fjola without speaking to Christer, the quest will proceed as if you had.

## Bugs

- If you kill Fjola after talking to her and obtaining her wedding band, then talk to her husband, the game will then update the quest to talk to Fjola again. However, since Fjola is dead, you cannot talk to her, and therefore can no longer complete the miscellaneous quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  - However, you can use the console to bring Fjola back and finish the quest. In console, type `prid 000430B5`, `moveto player`, and `resurrect 1` then talk to her.
- If you choose to tell Christer that you did not find Fjola, her corpse might spawn in the first hall left of Christer. The quest is then impossible to complete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- If you decide to kill Christer, upon killing him, the quest will complete. If you then return to Fjola, she still says *"I didn't expect to see you again. What became of my doting husband?"*.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Despite promising you gold, Christer never gives you any, regardless of how you complete the quest.
- Sometimes when you speak to Christer he will only have generic comments and not offer you the quest. Attempting the following command lines to manually fix it does not appear to work: `setstage` to 5, 10, or 11, `disable`/`enable`, and `resetAI`. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Mistwatch (dunMistwatchQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 11 |  | *Objective 11:* Search Mistwatch for Fjola |
| 75 |  | *Objective 75:* Return to Christer |
| 80 |  | *Objective 75:* Return to Christer |
| 90 |  | *Objective 85:* Report back to Fjola |
| 100 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 10, 70, 85, 89, 95.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunMistwatchQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunMistwatchQST`.

# Skyrim:Mistwatch

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Mistwatch ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Mistwatch "Lore:Mistwatch")) | | |
| # of Zones | 3 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Mistwatch Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit"), [Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MistwatchExterior01, MistwatchExterior02, MistwatchExterior03, Mistwatch01, Mistwatch02, Mistwatch03 | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") Northwest of [Northwind Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Mine "Skyrim:Northwind Mine") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Mistwatch

**Mistwatch** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing the [Mistwatch Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") and their [leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). It contains three zones: *[Mistwatch North Tower](#Mistwatch_North_Tower)*, *[Mistwatch West Tower](#Mistwatch_West_Tower)*, and *[Mistwatch East Tower](#Mistwatch_East_Tower)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)")**: Help [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").

### Exterior

To reach the fort, travel southeast along the road from [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"). After it crosses the bridge over the waterfalls south of Darkwater Crossing, the road starts to climb to the east. Partway up is a path to the north, with an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") on the ground to the left. The northern path will lead you to the entrance to the courtyard, though beware leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") on the path.

As you approach the fort, unless you are successfully [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), you will be warned to stay away by the four leveled Mistwatch Bandits that patrol the outer walls of the fort. To reach the courtyard, you can approach from the northeast or southwest; both approaches pass under arches. To the left of the northeastern arch there is a flight of stone stairs leading up to the top of the outer wall. At the top, beside the ruined tower, is a wooden table with a random [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") on it. North of the ruined tower is an intact tower with two doorways, one facing south and the other west. Inside the tower is a circular room containing several long wooden tables and benches with a total of four bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and three bottles of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") on and around the tables. The rest of the walls are empty with the exception of a lever to the left of a wooden bridge section, which will drop both halves of a wooden drawbridge that was built to replace a collapsed stone bridge. Dropping the bridge will allow access to the interior of the fort, comprising a set of sequential towers built into the mountainside.

### Mistwatch North Tower

Entering the first tower leads into a wide, curved corridor with a wooden door at the end and a doorway on the left. There is a small table on the right holding a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). As you approach the doorway, you will hear a farmer by the name of [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer"). If you talk to him, he will ask you to help him by searching for his wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). If you agree, the miscellaneous quest [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)") will start, and he will give you a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Key "Skyrim:Mistwatch Key") that opens all the doors in the fort. There is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in the same room as him, along with a couple food barrels and a set of shelves holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), an empty random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack. The wooden door at the end of the corridor is locked and requires the key Christer gives you to open.

Through the door is a large circular room with an opening to the north. In the room are two unowned bedrolls and a dresser containing random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") near the west wall, while opposite is a long wooden table with three [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") on it, with five more pheasants hanging from racks above the table. Beyond the opening there is an empty cart on your right and a stairwell curving up around the inside of the tower. There are a couple bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the stairs as you climb. On the landing partway up are three [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"). A bandit patrols the top half of these stairs, and a magic-using bandit can be found in another circular room at the top. This room contains a pair of cupboards holding a random enchanted [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a random potion of stamina, a random poison, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). To the right of these is a long wooden table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a kettle containing two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). There is a hanging rack above the table holding two bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). To the west is a level-locked gate to a cell that contains two hay piles and some ragged robes. The lock to the cell isn't opened by the key received from Christer. To the right of the cell is an unowned single bed, with an unlocked chest against the northeast wall. Between the bed and chest is an alcove with a ladder up to a level-locked trapdoor that can be unlocked with the key given to you by Christer, leading to *[Mistwatch Lower Balcony](#Exterior:_Mistwatch_Lower_Balcony)*.

### Exterior: Mistwatch Lower Balcony

Outside is a lean-to with an unowned bedroll under it and a campfire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging over it. A path leads to a level-locked door into *[Mistwatch West Tower](#Mistwatch_West_Tower)*; however, before entering, continue past the door to find an adept-locked chest.

### Mistwatch West Tower

As you enter this tower, there is another curved corridor with a set of shelves on the right holding a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). To the left are several unowned single beds against the walls, with two bandits roaming this level. There are also three tables holding a total of five bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat"). There is an unlocked cell along the left wall, with a [dead Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)") lying on the ground inside and shackles on the rear wall with blood splattered on the wall below, suggesting how the prisoner met her end. To the left of the cell is an unlocked chest, while to the right on a small square table is a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_(Mistwatch) "Skyrim:Note (Mistwatch)") which gives more details about how she died. Opposite the cell is a set of shelves holding a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), a couple bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and several pieces of cheese. Farther along the corridor to the west is another curving flight of stairs leading up to the next floor. There are two more bandits as you climb, one partway up and the other at the top. The corridor continues circling the tower, passing a long wooden table against the inside wall holding a quiver of random arrows, a couple bulbs of garlic, two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), with a second drum under the table. Continuing around, before the door at the end is another table with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. The door is level-locked and leads out onto *[Mistwatch Higher Balcony](#Exterior:_Mistwatch_Higher_Balcony)*.

### Exterior: Mistwatch Higher Balcony

Apart from the trapdoor leading out of *Mistwatch West Tower* and a path across to the door into *[Mistwatch East Tower](#Mistwatch_East_Tower)*, there is nothing else of interest.

### Mistwatch East Tower

The east tower is the highest tower and home to Fjola, the bandit leader and wife of Christer. The door to this tower can only be unlocked if you have the key given to you by Christer. Entering leads into another typical tower, with a corridor curving off to the right and a set of shelves opposite holding three [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), some random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). To the right is a second set of shelves against the inner wall holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an iron helmet, a pair of [Stormcloak officer boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Boots "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Boots"), a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), four loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and seven common books. As you approach the end of the corridor, you will encounter the friendly bandit leader, Fjola (see the [quest page](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)") for details regarding all options available at this point).

Past Fjola, the corridor leads into a central circular room with two cells and a room to the west. Both cells are empty and contain only unowned bedrolls. There is a long wooden table in the main room with a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and four loose coins on top. The western room has an unowned single bed against the north wall, while opposite is a dresser containing random clothes and a row of three weapon racks holding a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") and a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons") [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"). On the dresser is a random potion of stamina, a common book, and a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Hallgerd's Tale](/wiki/Skyrim:Hallgerd%27s_Tale "Skyrim:Hallgerd's Tale")*. Finally, hanging from a rack in the southwestern corner of the bedroom area are two rabbits.

There is no shortcut back to Christer, except down the side of the mountain. Fast traveling to Mistwatch places you at the lowest level, so this may be helpful in getting back to him.

## Notes

- The Mistwatch Bandits wear better quality [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") and [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and carry far more gold than typical [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), lending weight to Fjola's claim that *"Now every free blade from here to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") wants to sign on for a piece."*
- It is possible to explore the rest of *Mistwatch North Tower* without starting the related quest if you drop down onto Mistwatch from the mountains behind it and enter through the trapdoor at the top of the tower. However, you will not be able to make it past the locked gate, and will therefore need to go back out through the trapdoor.
- You can enter and speak with the bandit boss without starting the related quest if you have the [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Wax_Key "Skyrim:Wax Key") [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") perk. Unlocking the master-locked door before the final tower gives you the Mistwach key, which then can be used to open and enter the last tower. Doing this will make all bandits inside and outside of the tower friendly.
- Mistwatch is marked as cleared when the related quest is completed, regardless of how you choose to complete the quest. Therefore, clearing this location can either be triggered by killing its boss enemy (i.e., the bandit leader), or by talking to her, convincing Christer to leave, and then returning to tell her that he is gone.
- The doors from within the tower to the outside have custom names, such as "Mistwatch Courtyard", "Mistwatch Lower Balcony", and "Mistwatch Higher Balcony", instead of the usual generic "Skyrim" name given to doors leading back outside.
- The towers offer excellent views of [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") to the north. A [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") circling the misty hill is a common sight.
- To the north is a ruined building covered in sulfur. Three [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") will rise here as you approach, but there is nothing else of note.
- A [frightened woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Frightened_Woman "Skyrim:Frightened Woman") who escaped the Mistwatch Bandits may be [encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Mistwatch_Escapee "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wild. She will mark Mistwatch on the map for you if you speak to her.
- Mistwatch also [appears](/wiki/Online:Mistwatch "Online:Mistwatch") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- One of the bandits on the lower level of *Mistwatch West Tower* may not be tagged as a Mistwatch Bandit, but just as a normal leveled [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- Clearing this location does not increment the number of "Dungeons Cleared" displayed in your journal, and therefore does not contribute to the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement.

  **Mod Notes**: The script for `dunMistwatchQST` (stage 100) uses the command `MistwatchLocation.SetCleared()`, which evidently only marks the place as cleared, but does not increment the other counters.

# Skyrim:Misty Grove

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Worldspace: Misty Grove  ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Misty_Grove "Lore:Misty Grove")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DA14Interior | |

Misty Grove

**Misty Grove** is one of the [Myriad Realms of Revelry](/wiki/Lore:Revelry "Lore:Revelry") created by [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine"), where he is holding a feast with some of his followers. It is only accessible through a magic portal found in [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") during the related quest.

The center of the grove

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Sam Guevenne](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne") / [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine")  [Commoners](/wiki/Skyrim:Commoner "Skyrim:Commoner") (8) |

## Related Quests

- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

### Misty Grove

The grove can only be reached once you have followed the clues to locate [Sam Guevenne](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne") during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"). You travel here by entering a portal inside [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar"). Upon being transported to the grove, you arrive at the beginning of a sunken path lit with lanterns spaced evenly along its length, with raised banks on both sides preventing you from straying too far from the fixed pathway. The path crosses and recrosses a burbling stream flowing from north to south, which also has raised banks. It always appears to be evening when you arrive. As you travel along the path, it is possible to catch a few [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug"), but the grove appears to contain no other creatures and no harvestable plants, flowers, or fungi. The path leads to a clearing prominently featuring a long table laid with a feast of four [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat"), four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). Around the table sit eight [commoners](/wiki/Skyrim:Commoner "Skyrim:Commoner") who are carousing and seem fairly deep in their cups; they wear a collection of common clothing, but don't carry any other items. There are two smaller tables beside the main table with small mead barrels on top, and strings of lanterns hanging overhead light the whole clearing. Finally, there is Sam Guevenne, who after conversation reveals himself to be the Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine"). He gives you his [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), and returns you to the inn where you first met and agreed to the competition. Any items you picked up while in the grove remain in your inventory when you return to the inn.

## Notes

- Sam Guevenne describes this place as one "where the wine flows like water".
- None of the items here are owned, thus making them free to take.

## Bugs

- If you return to Morvunskar after completing A Night To Remember, sometimes the portal to Misty Grove will still be accessible. Passing through it will end with you being stuck in Misty Grove, as Sanguine is no longer there to teleport you out.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - Reload a save from before you entered.
  -  On the PC, you can open the console and type `tcl` to toggle collision, then fly under the map just below where you enter Misty Grove to find a door that will take you back to Morvunskar.

## Maps

- 

  Misty Grove

# Skyrim:Mixwater Mill

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Wood Mill.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Wood_Mill.png) | Wood Mill: Mixwater Mill ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mixwater+Mill)) | | |
