Mixwater Mill

**Mixwater Mill** is a [lumber mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Mills "Skyrim:Wood Mills") on the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and southeast of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock").

[Gilfre](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre "Skyrim:Gilfre") has lived here alone since her five workers left to fight in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gilfre](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre "Skyrim:Gilfre") |

## Related Quests

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 2 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  2 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  1 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") | 4 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 3 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Mixwater Mill

Along with the sawmill itself is [Gilfre's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre%27s_House "Skyrim:Gilfre's House") and the now empty [Worker's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Worker%27s_House "Skyrim:Worker's House"). Gilfre's residence holds a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")* (for full details, see the dedicated [house page](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre%27s_House "Skyrim:Gilfre's House")). All items inside the worker's house can be freely taken (for full details, see the dedicated [house page](/wiki/Skyrim:Worker%27s_House "Skyrim:Worker's House")). The [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") is next to the sawmill, and the [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") is in front of the fireplace inside Gilfre's house.

The mill can serve as a useful free home if you marry Gilfre. However, the drying salmon and containers outside Gilfre's house do not become player-owned, even after marriage, and looting them will be considered stealing, though the [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") remains free to take. You can also freely sleep in the worker's house.

With [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, you can buy [sawn logs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") by speaking to Gilfre. You can also cut your own logs for free if she has given you permission to do so or if you have married her. A [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found here as well.

With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") creation installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found by the water, along with a small box containing five [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") and some [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales").

# Skyrim:Moesring Pass

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Pass.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Pass.png) | Pass: Moesring Pass ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Moesring+Pass)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Occupants | |
| [Rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2MoesringPass01, DLC2MoesringPassExterior01, DLC2MoesringPassExterior02 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Northwest of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak") East-northeast of [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz") | |

Moesring Pass

**Moesring Pass** is a mountain [pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Places#Passes "Skyrim:Dragonborn Places") due northwest of the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak"), inhabited by [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") guarding the nearby Strange Vessel.

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

## Moesring Pass

The pass

Rieklings have made camp at this pass high in the mountains. It is the junction of three paths, with the Strange Vessel in the middle, and is home to four rieklings, including one mounted on a [bristleback](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback"). One riekling walkway overlooks paths from the south and the southwest, and a second walkway bridges a path from the northwest. Three lookout towers are built into the ends of the walkways, with the tallest tower directly west of the Strange Vessel. Two rieklings are on the walkways, with a third slightly farther to the southwest hidden in a bush. The mounted riekling is farther uphill to the north beside a campfire.

There is a mounted elk head in a cart in the middle of the pass. On the head is a [chitin helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Helmet "Skyrim:Chitin Helmet") and a [cave bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"). A few paces east of the cart is a [riekling hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut"), with a sack to the left of the entrance. To the north is an end table on its side, with an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") on top and a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") beside it. Farther uphill is the campfire, with a kettle next to it containing a fillet of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"). Behind the fire is a riekling tent containing a [bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt"), a [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(weapon) "Skyrim:Knife (weapon)"), and a sack. To the left of the tent is another riekling hut. To the south of the fire are three barrels; one barrel holds an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), the next a piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") and a [fork](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(weapon) "Skyrim:Fork (weapon)"), and the third a belted tunic. Finally, to the right of the door into the Strange Vessel is a sack.

## Strange Vessel

Inside the strange vessel

Inside, you can clearly see the vessel is upside down. It appears to be of Dwemer construction, with riekling paintings covering everything. It is lit by a goat horn on a stand beside the door and by a typical Dwemer light on what is now the floor. Along the eastern wall are crates, barrels, and an unlocked chest. On the floor is a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes"), a pair of leather boots, and a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"). South of the entrance is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). Behind the skeleton is a flight of stairs that can't be used, behind which is an adept-locked chest and another barrel.

## Notes

- The vessel itself is probably the [Patchwork Airship](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Patchwork_Airship "Bloodmoon:Patchwork Airship"), though it has suffered more damage from the elements since its first appearance in [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon") over 200 years ago.
- Following the downhill path to the southwest leads to an [unmarked place](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Unmarked Places"): a [shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") with another [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") beside it.

## Bugs

- Followers may not be able to navigate Mosering Pass properly due to a bad section of navmesh.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Moldering Ruins

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Dwelling.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Dwelling.png) | Nordic Dwelling: Moldering Ruins ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moldering+Ruins+%28DG%29)) | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), [Vampire Thralls](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire Thrall"), [Death Hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound"), dead [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") | |

| DLC1MolderingRuins01 | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |

| West of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") East of [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Moldering Ruins

**Moldering Ruins** is a small [camp and concealed cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") west of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains only one zone, *[Moldering Ruins](#Moldering_Ruins)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**: Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The camp consists of two small tents (each with a bedroll), a campfire, and one large tent. Several [death hounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Hound "Skyrim:Death Hound") and/or [vampire's thralls](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall") will be around the camp. The large tent contains several random items on a table, including a damage health [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), a health/magicka/stamina [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), some leveled [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), and a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") (both up to Elven). Underneath the table is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Against the rear of the tent are several crates and barrels, a couple of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks, and a [coffin](/wiki/Skyrim:Coffin "Skyrim:Coffin"), with a trapdoor at the southern end of the tent. It leads down into the cave section of Moldering Ruins.

### Moldering Ruins

Interior

Upon using the trapdoor, you enter into a small circular room with a tunnel in front of you descending a flight of stairs to the south. There are five [hanging mosses](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing in this first room. At the bottom of the stairs you enter a badly damaged room with rubble all around. A vampire's thrall and a leveled vampire boss will attack as soon as you are detected.

There is a stone table on your left in an alcove against the east wall with two dead draugr, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a [skeever tail](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), and a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") on top, and a second burial urn underneath. There are a couple of empty coffins, a few more hanging mosses, and several opened sarcophagi along both the east and west side walls; some of the draugr may get raised during the fight. There are a couple of large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") along the east wall, and halfway along the west wall is a set of shelves holding a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a salt pile, and a burial urn. There is another burial urn and a partially buried [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") at the rear of the room against the south wall, on a ledge above the floor that can be reached by following either of the side walls and then climbing the rubble until you reach the end. Stairs descend on either side of a large carved piece of stone to a lower level with a bedroll on the left side; farther to the rear on the right side over a gap is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and a couple of food sacks along with a few unusable barrels and a unique but worthless [bloody tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloody_Tankard "Skyrim:Bloody Tankard"). At the very bottom is a campfire in a brazier with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") balanced on the edge. To the south of the fire is a partially buried unlocked chest between a partially buried dead draugr and another large urn.

## Notes

- Moldering Ruins does not appear to have been created for a specific purpose. The only reason any other content added by *Dawnguard* will send you here is because the ruin was added to the preexisting random-selection lists.
-  Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") assigns Moldering Ruins to [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") instead.

## Maps

- 

  Moldering Ruins

# Skyrim:Moorside Inn

## Overview

Moorside Inn

**Moorside Inn** is the only [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). It is owned and run by [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna"), from whom you may rent a room for 10 gold per night. Food can also be purchased and sold here. [Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk") is the inn's bard, although his performances are [not popular](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk"). Business seems slow, if not nonexistent, as Jonna will tell you that the front door doesn't get much use. One of the few regular visitors is [Gorm](/wiki/Skyrim:Gorm "Skyrim:Gorm"), who comes in every evening for his dinner.

[Hroggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroggar "Skyrim:Hroggar")'s burned-down house is found next to Moorside Inn.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Eisa Blackthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa_Blackthorn "Skyrim:Eisa Blackthorn") †  [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk") |

† If she survives during [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Lurbuk "Skyrim:Kill Lurbuk")**: Silence a [terrible bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk"), permanently.

### Exterior

There are two separate flights of stairs leading up to the porch on the front of the inn. Behind the inn against the wall are two patches of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen") that can be harvested.

### Moorside Inn

The common room inside the Moorside Inn.

Through the door, you enter the main common room of the inn, with the counter at the far end; [Jonna](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonna "Skyrim:Jonna") can usually be found behind it. There are five long wooden tables and benches against the walls of the room. Four of the tables hold a couple loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and several bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). The table on your right as you enter also holds two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and pieces of cheese. In the center of the room is a fire pit. There are several barrels of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") found around the room, mainly in the corners. There are three chairs at the northeast end of the room, which is normally where [Lurbuk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurbuk "Skyrim:Lurbuk") plies his trade, except late at night when he retires to the first room on the left to sleep.

There are three doorways leading to three bedrooms, two to the southeast and a larger room to the northwest. There are more pieces of cheese and bottles of wine and alto wine on the counter and under it. Also under the counter are three small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe"), plenty of bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a copy of *[The Windhelm Letters](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Windhelm_Letters "Skyrim:The Windhelm Letters")*. Against the northwest wall, on either side of the doorway to the larger bedroom, are two sets of shelves holding three [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), four loaves of bread, seven bottles of Nord mead, six bottles of wine, and two bottles of alto wine. Behind the counter are three hanging racks with six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and ten [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from them, and between them are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, an elves ear, and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from a beam. Behind all of this is a row of vats.

The first bedroom on the left that Lurbuk generally uses consists of a single owned bed in the eastern corner, next to which is a round table and chair holding a common book and a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). At the foot of the bed is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and to the left of the doorway is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). The second bedroom consists of a single unowned bed in the southern corner, a round wooden table and chair next to it, and a dresser against the southwest wall holding four common books, while inside a basket is a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Racial Phylogeny](/wiki/Skyrim:Racial_Phylogeny "Skyrim:Racial Phylogeny")*.

The larger bedroom consists of a large double bed in the middle of the northwest wall, with dressers on either side holding a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of Nord mead, a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), and six common books. On the floor, beside the dresser on the right, is a large coin purse. Along the northeast wall are a pile of food sacks and a long unlocked chest. To the right of the doorway is a wooden table and chair holding a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). This is the room you will be given if you decide to pay to stay the night.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 4 | Bottles of [Honningbrew Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") |
| 10 | Random inn [Food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |
| 7 | Random [beverages](/wiki/Skyrim:Beverages "Skyrim:Beverages") |

Mor Khazgur Cellar

**Mor Khazgur Cellar** is a cellar located in the [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") stronghold of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur") behind the [Mor Khazgur Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Larak%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Larak's Longhouse").

Down in the cellar

## Mor Khazgur Cellar

Upon entering via the novice-locked trapdoor, you look down a sloping passage that appears as a natural cave rather than a normal cellar. On the left-hand side of this passage are three [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") mushrooms. The passage opens into a room with a central pillar. To the left is a wicker fence enclosing a mushroom patch of two [blisterworts](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), four [bleeding crowns](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), two [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and two more fly amanitas. Next is an iron drying rack from which hang two braids of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and one [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"). To the right of this are three food barrels and three covered baskets. To the right again is another iron drying rack from which hang a dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and another dried elves ear. Next is an adept-locked jail door to a small room with a single shelving unit. The top shelf holds a [potion of the healer](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Healer "Skyrim:Potion of the Healer"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a random skill potion. The second shelf has a [minor healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a leveled [strength potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), and a random leveled skill potion. To the right of the jail door are some [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") and a chest containing some minor loot. Next on the east wall is another shelving unit with three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the top shelf and three bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the bottom.
